<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Please note that Jean Girard was the owner, and maybe one of the copyists of that manuscript, probably NOT the composer. All the pieces are unidentified in the manuscript; however, 16 pieces have been attributed with certainty to Nicolas LeBègue.
</p>
